The MacKay solo run (*Black Cat* vol. 1 #1–12, 2019–2020; vol. 2 #1–10, 2020–2021; and the *King in Black: Black Cat* and *Giant-Size Black Cat* tie-ins) is, in our view, the most psychologically *legible* period of her adult life. For the first time in the canonical record she is depicted living a continuous, daily existence rather than appearing as a plot vector in someone else's title. The forensic content of those issues — apartment, wardrobe, fence relationships, breakfast habits, who she calls first when something goes wrong — fills in the granular life-pattern the rest of the file had to infer.

**The crew.** Bruno Grainger, driver and muscle, functions as a younger brother she protects reflexively; Doctor Korpse, technical specialist, occupies the role of in-house craftsman she defers to on his domain; the elder Black Fox is the *father she chose* once the biological father became unavailable to the role — a master thief whose competence she respects and whose mortality she now actively manages. The structure is significant: she has organized her professional life into a kinship-shaped unit. This is a woman who lost the original family to crime and prison and has reassembled the topology in adulthood with herself in the parental seat. The MacKay run shows her bailing crew out of jams she did not need to enter, paying medical bills, mediating disputes, and refusing scores that would have endangered them — behavior consistent with the maternal-mentor profile flagged in §3, now operationalized.

**The opposition turned counterpart.** Odessa Drake, head of the Thieves Guild, occupies an interesting slot in the current period: rival, occasional employer, intermittent lover, and the only woman in the file who has functioned as a peer-equal in Felicia's professional life. The Drake relationship demonstrates something the dossier should weight: Felicia's relational pattern is not exclusively cross-sex. With Drake the same grammar holds — approach via theatrical risk, intimacy as transaction, withdrawal at the threshold of being known — but absent the index-trauma valence of male partners. The Drake material is the cleanest depiction we have of her relational style operating *outside* the PTSD circuit, and it is informative: the pattern persists. The avoidance is therefore not exclusively trauma-driven; it has become characterological infrastructure regardless of the partner's sex.

**The craft.** The MacKay arcs depict heists for their own sake — the Wakandan-tech vault, the Quentin Beck estate, the Black Fox legacy job, the King in Black-era infiltrations. These are not need-driven jobs. She is, by mid-run, financially comfortable in a way that retires the *means* explanation for her continued operation. What remains is the *aesthetic* explanation: she steals because the heist is the form her selfhood takes. The activity is not symptomatic. It is constitutive. Any future intervention frame that treats the burglary as the problem to be eliminated will fail; the burglary is the load-bearing structure of an otherwise compensated trauma adaptation.

---

## 3. The Reconnection Cycle with Peter Parker

The Wells *Amazing Spider-Man* run ("Heist," #10–14 of vol. 6, and the surrounding material) refreshes the Peter axis after a long fallow period. The depicted reconnection is instructive precisely because it is **not** a reconciliation. They cooperate on a job involving the Black Fox's debt to a third party; they flirt in the established grammar; they do not resume a relationship. The Wells material shows Felicia in what we would now call her *stabilized default*: warm with Peter, undefended for short intervals, candid about the prior history, and unwilling to reopen the romantic frame. This is the healthiest depicted Peter-state on file. She no longer needs him to validate the persona (the MacKay run gave her a crew that does); she does not need to test him (Superior tested him and the results are filed); and she has stopped using the relationship as a primary affect regulator.

The MJ adjacency in the same period is worth noting. Felicia interacts with Mary Jane civilly across recent appearances — no longer threatened, no longer competitive — which is a measurable change from the late-DeFalco and Aguirre-Sacasa eras. The change reads as evidence that the Peter-fixation has been demoted from a primary attachment to a *historically important secondary*, freeing relational bandwidth for the crew, for Drake, and — importantly — for herself.

---

## 4. Domestic and Operational Pattern: The Daily File

Granular life-pattern across the most recent depicted period, compiled from environmental detail across the MacKay, Wells, and ancillary runs:

- **Residence.** Multiple. The depicted primary is a converted upper-floor apartment in a non-doorman building in lower Manhattan — security retrofitted by Korpse, two egress routes minimum (one through the building, one across rooftops), no formal lease in her legal name. Secondary safehouses in at least two outer boroughs and one upstate. Surveillance file would flag her near-total avoidance of buildings with biometric entry, doorman logs, or package-delivery cameras as routine she handles, not paranoia.
- **Wardrobe.** Two strict registers. *Operational*: the suit, masks, low-signature street kit (dark, well-cut, nothing branded loudly). *Civilian*: expensive but not flashy, runs to tailored leather, fitted denim, cashmere; jewelry minimal and rotated. She does not wear repeat outfits to repeat venues — a counter-recognition habit that has become aesthetic preference.
- **Diet and routine.** Light, regular, athlete-style. Coffee black, morning training maintained as non-negotiable, no skipped strength work. Social drinking — wine with meals, cocktails in seduction-frame settings — never alone to excess. No depicted morning-after consequences across the recent period. The somatic discipline is intact.
- **Sleep.** Depicted as light. Wakes fully and instantly. Sleeps alone by strong preference even with current partners; the few depicted overnight sequences end with her dressed and out before the partner wakes. This is not narrative shorthand; it is a stable behavioral feature.
- **Communication.** Burner phones, rotated. Signal-discipline taught to the crew and enforced. She maintains a small number of long-relationship contacts (fences, forgers, one or two cops on the take, the Foreigner as a strictly arms-length back-channel) and refreshes the operational layer aggressively.
- **Money.** Diversified — cash, art, gems, a small number of legitimate-front holdings. The MacKay run implies real estate. She does not appear to bank in her legal name in any meaningful volume.
- **Self-soothing rituals.** Long baths (depicted), rooftop running (depicted, non-operational), the deliberate selection and study of a target weeks before a job (depicted across multiple arcs — the planning *is* the regulation, not just preparation for the job). The aesthetic-pleasure channel flagged in §5 is the primary non-relational regulator.

---

## 5. The Symbiote Period and the Body-Modification Pattern

Across the recent King in Black material and subsequent tie-ins, Felicia bonded briefly with a symbiote. The episode is short and not central, but it is diagnostically significant in the file's longitudinal frame. This is the **second** time she has accepted a non-trivial body modification under conditions of perceived inadequacy to a peer (the first being the Kingpin's luck field). The pattern is now confirmed: under pressure she will alter her own body to be operationally adequate, will conceal or minimize the alteration to those closest to her, and will experience shame and physical disengagement on the back end of it. Any future scenario presenting her with a body-modification offer under partner-comparison stress should be treated as a known vulnerability vector.

---

## 6. The Black Fox and the Anticipated Loss

The current period has foregrounded the elder Black Fox's age and mortality in a way the earlier canon did not. He functions, as noted, as the chosen-father slot. Felicia's depicted behavior around him — protective beyond operational need, willing to take jobs whose only function is to settle his debts, present at convalescence — is unusually undefended for her. The file should anticipate that his eventual death (whether on-page or off) will be the most significant attachment loss she has yet sustained on the longitudinal record, exceeding the cumulative Peter losses because the Fox occupies a developmental slot the Peter relationship never quite filled. Decompensation risk in the year following any such loss is non-trivial. Predicted form: not a return to the post-Superior gang configuration but a withdrawal into solitary operations of escalating risk — the *control-the-conditions-of-vulnerability* drive turned inward and inflated.

---

## 7. Current Integration and Residual Pattern

The present-state read, holding all of the above: Felicia is, by her own standards and by ours, in the most integrated configuration of her adult life. The PTSD remains compensated. The cold-operator self-state remains contingently accessible and has been activated once in the recent past under known precipitants. The Peter relationship is demoted and stable. The crew functions as a chosen family that is meeting attachment needs the romantic axis historically did not meet. The aesthetic life is rich and self-generated. The ethical code is self-authored and consistently held — don't hurt civilians, steal beautifully, protect the circle, never the frame-violator. She is laundering competence into mentorship; she is laundering trauma into craft; and she is, in middle adulthood, doing the work that adolescence and early adulthood made structurally impossible for her.

**Residual pattern, undiminished.** She still sleeps alone by morning. She still flirts as default register with anyone she perceives as a competence-peer. She still does not have a civilian future plan and shows no interest in constructing one. She still cannot tolerate sentimentality from a casual partner without bolting. She still controls the unmasking — physical and psychological — at all times and in all rooms. She still refers to herself in costume name in self-talk. The mask is still, by her account and by her behavior, the truth.

**Where she is now.** Operating out of New York. Crew intact. Solvent. Romantically uncommitted by choice and apparently at peace with it. On terms with Spider-Man that are warmer than they have been in twenty years of internal chronology and contain no expectation of resumption. Aware of her own pattern in a way she was not at twenty-five — the MacKay-era internal monologue depicts genuine, non-defended self-knowledge in private moments — and choosing the pattern anyway, which is the difference between symptom and identity.

**How she got here.** By surviving the index trauma; by building a persona that worked; by losing and reacquiring it under the Superior injury; by being given, finally, a title of her own in which to inhabit a life rather than serve a plot; by finding a crew that did the attachment work the Peter axis could not; by aging into the maternal-mentor slot that her own nineteen-year-old self had needed and not been given; and by doing — slowly, in private, on her own terms, with no clinician and no program — the integration work that her structure allowed her to do.

The file as of the present interval reads: stable, compensated, productive, contingent. Watch the Fox. Watch for body-modification offers under peer-comparison stress. Watch for sexual humiliation events. Otherwise — observe and respect the construction. It is hers, it works, and the cost of dismantling it would exceed the cost of leaving it intact.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — FELICIA HARDY (BLACK CAT)
## SECTION: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Scope: full somatic record from infancy through current operational period. Includes constitutional baseline, developmental milestones inferable from competence, documented injuries, iatrogenic modifications, gynecological/sexual health, substance exposure, sleep and metabolic patterns, and the psychological correlate of each entry. Source material drawn primarily from* Amazing Spider-Man *(Wolfman, DeFalco, Michelinie, Slott, Spencer, Wells eras),* Spectacular Spider-Man, Web of Spider-Man, *the Smith/Dodson* Evil That Men Do *miniseries, Aguirre-Sacasa's* Sensational Spider-Man, *Waid's* Daredevil, *Bendis/Maleev* Daredevil, *MacKay's* Black Cat *solo (2019–2021), and Slott's* Superior Spider-Man*. Where canon is silent, inferences are flagged as such and built from somatic logic (training load, injury pattern, depicted recovery times).*

---

### 1. CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

Northern European descent, white phenotype; the striking platinum hair is natural and present from at least adolescent depictions, not dyed (consistent across all artists, never retconned as bleach despite obvious convenience for such a retcon). Eye color green. Adult height in the low-to-mid 170s of centimeters; weight in the high-50s to low-60s of kilograms at operational condition — a gymnast/middleweight-fighter body composition rather than a powerlifter or sprinter build. No depicted disfigurements, congenital anomalies, or chronic dermatological issues. Skin notably unmarked across decades despite the volume of combat and rooftop work, which itself is data: she heals well, conditions tissue carefully, and her work — when uninterrupted — depends on *not getting hit*.

**Childhood medical (inferred, late-1960s through mid-1970s).** Upper-middle-class to wealthy upbringing in Queens; access to full pediatric care. Walter Hardy's clandestine wealth and the family's outward presentation as a successful business household imply complete vaccination, regular dental, pediatric orthodontic work consistent with the symmetrical adult dentition (no dental anomalies depicted even in close-up Dodson, Campbell, or Romita Jr. work). No depicted childhood hospitalizations. Father's frequent "business travel" — actually multi-week burglary tours and at least one prolonged incarceration period concealed from her — likely correlates with a period of mild somatic complaints in latency (the standard pediatric-stress repertoire: stomachaches, headaches, sleep onset difficulty), unrecorded but consistent with the personality structure that emerges later.

**Adolescent physical development.** Apparently uneventful. The competitive athletics that show up in the college period (gymnastics first, multiple martial arts second) presuppose a sustained pre-college movement history — early ballet or gymnastics is the only path to the level of axial control she demonstrates in her twenties. The body she later weaponizes was being prepared, without that purpose, throughout childhood. This is biographically poignant: the asset that saved her existed because of a privileged childhood that also taught her she was safe.

---

### 2. THE INDEX TRAUMA — FRESHMAN YEAR, EMPIRE STATE UNIVERSITY

*Source:* Spider-Man/Black Cat: The Evil That Men Do *(Smith/Dodson, 2002–06).*

Sexual assault by her then-boyfriend Ryan during her freshman year. Mechanism, per canon: a non-stranger rape in a domestic setting, no weapon depicted, physical injury limited and non-disabling. There is no in-canon record of acute medical follow-up — no rape kit, no hospital — which is consistent with the early-1980s (or modernized equivalent) collegiate environment and with her personality structure: the disclosure pathway closed almost immediately and she pivoted to private remediation. The decision not to seek medical care is itself an injury, because it forecloses both the forensic record that might have permitted prosecution and the therapeutic record that might have entered her into a treatment system.

**Direct somatic sequelae (depicted or strongly implied):**
- Acute startle response and hypervigilance, never fully extinguished, later operationalized as professional skill.
- Aversion to specific somatic configurations — being pinned, being approached from behind by an unknown party, being held without consent even playfully. Her in-costume fight choreography across decades shows a consistent preference for *not letting the opponent close to grappling range from behind*; she will accept a frontal clinch she controls, but spins out of any rear engagement with disproportionate urgency.
- Probable transient menstrual irregularity in the months following (inferred from the typical neuroendocrine response to acute trauma; not depicted).
- Sleep architecture disrupted in this period (inferred; not depicted).

**The training response.** Within weeks she began a deliberate physical-reconstruction program: gymnastics retained and intensified, then karate, judo, and at least two additional striking/throwing arts. This was not therapy — it was target preparation. She intended to find Ryan and kill him. Medically, this period laid down the musculoskeletal and neural foundation of every subsequent capability: the dense proprioceptive map, the conditioned reflex arcs, the cardiovascular base. Training intensity at the level required would have produced the standard injuries of the path — repeated joint sprains, at least one stress reaction in a metatarsal or tibia, mat burns, callused knuckles and feet, recurrent low-grade tendinopathy in the wrists from break-falls. None are depicted; all are inferable.

**The catharsis that didn't happen.** Ryan died in a drunk-driving accident before she completed her preparation. The mobilized vengeance had no terminus. This is the single most consequential *non-event* in her medical file because the body had been organized around a discharge that never occurred, and the organization persisted. The costumed-thief identity is, in part, a chronic motor-program looking for its original target.

---

### 3. THE FATHER'S INCARCERATION AND THE OPERATIONAL DEBUT

The decision to break Walter Hardy out of prison (*ASM* #194–195) commits her body to operational risk for the first time. Across the early Wolfman/Pollard and DeFalco/Frenz arcs she sustains the standard professional-burglar attrition: rope burns from rapid rappels, repeated minor lacerations from broken glass and metalwork during entry, bruising from fights with Spider-Man (who calibrates force downward against her but is still superhumanly strong — every contact leaves a mark). She is depicted limping briefly after the first major engagement and is not depicted again until clearly recovered, which is the canon-typical compression of a multi-week healing arc into a panel transition.

---

### 4. THE LUCK-POWERS PROCEDURE — IATROGENIC MODIFICATION

*Source:* Amazing Spider-Man *#220s, revealed* #245 *(O'Neil/Mooney era); side-effect arc through* #270s–280s; *removal by Doctor Strange in the late Michelinie run.*

This is the most medically consequential event in her adult file and the only formal body modification on record.

**The procedure.** Kingpin's biotechnical apparatus performed an unspecified surgical/chemical intervention that conferred a probability-field effect — adverse luck radiating outward to those in proximity to her, particularly those targeting her or her allies. The procedure was performed under conditions of emotional duress: she had concluded that she was Spider-Man's inferior in raw capability and that the relationship would not survive that disparity. She consented; she did not negotiate; she did not seek a second opinion.

**Acute medical considerations (inferable).** Any procedure capable of producing a sustained probabilistic field effect must have involved either (a) a deep neuroendocrine intervention, (b) a sub-cellular modification with broad somatic distribution, or (c) implanted hardware with no depicted surgical scarring (which would imply elite surgical technique consistent with Kingpin's resources). No scars are depicted. Recovery period in canon: compressed but non-trivial — she is briefly out of operation. She conceals the procedure from Peter completely.

**Functional behavior of the field.** Initially appeared to function only when directed at adversaries. Later revealed (per Michelinie) to backwash onto loved ones — Peter specifically suffered repeated near-misses, accidents, and tactical reverses that were traceable to her presence. The field was not under conscious control at the granular level; it was constitutive, not voluntary.

**Removal.** Doctor Strange surgically (magically) excised the modification. No depicted somatic damage from removal. The psychological damage was the operative injury: she had altered her body to be adequate to a partner, and the alteration had wounded him, and the wound was discovered before she could disclose it on her own terms.

**Long-term consequences.**
- Loss of confidence in her own native capability briefly post-removal; she demonstrably re-trains and re-establishes baseline.
- A specific shame-marker that recurs across decades whenever a partner offers her something she suspects is a test of her sufficiency — she becomes evasive, deflects with humor, and refuses the offer even when it would benefit her. This pattern is visible from the Foreigner arcs onward.
- A persistent, low-grade somatic distrust: she relies on the body she trained, not on any enhancement, and is openly suspicious of "gifts" that promise capability. In the MacKay run she repeatedly declines artifacts that would augment her, preferring tools she has mastered.

**Notable later returns of the motif.** In several arcs (the Pulse-era Daredevil work; isolated *Marvel Knights* appearances; an arc in the MacKay solo) the luck-field manifests transiently — sometimes attributed to residual effect, sometimes to other agents (the Mephisto-adjacent retcons, the brief reactivation by the Black Fox's stolen artifact). Each return is treated by Felicia as a recurrence of an old illness — wary, contained, not celebrated. This is the somatic memory of an unwanted graft.

---

### 5. INJURY LEDGER — CHRONOLOGICAL, NOTABLE EVENTS

**Early Spider-Man arcs (1979–1984).** Multiple soft-tissue injuries during the courtship-combat period; one depicted fall of consequence (ASM #205-era) that she walks off but should not have. The pattern of walking off injuries that ought to immobilize her establishes early: she will not be seen recovering. Recovery happens off-panel and alone, which is significant — she does not have a treating relationship with any medical professional in canon, ever. There is no doctor in her file.

**Mid-1980s, DeFalco/Frenz/Michelinie era.** Repeated combat injuries during joint operations with Spider-Man. Of note: the cumulative concussive load from this period is non-trivial. She is struck head-and-neck on multiple occasions, including by superhumanly strong opponents (Doctor Octopus' tentacles glancingly, the Sin-Eater arc peripherally, multiple street-level enforcers). No diagnosed traumatic brain injury in canon; the absence of a clinical diagnosis does not mean absence of pathology. Her later vulnerability to certain kinds of disorientation under pressure (the Otto incident; specific moments in the MacKay run where her timing falters under emotional load) is consistent with subclinical cumulative concussive sequelae.

**The Foreigner period (Web of Spider-Man #1 forward, late 1980s).** Combat training intensifies; injury rate increases; she is involved in at least one operation involving live firearms exchange and demonstrates by-then-reflexive cover and movement discipline. No documented gunshot wounds in this period.

**1990s solo and team appearances.** Sporadic; injury record consistent with continued professional attrition. One depicted significant injury during a Kaine-adjacent encounter (Clone Saga peripheral); recovery off-panel.

**Bendis/Maleev *Daredevil* arc (early 2000s).** Sexual involvement with Matt Murdock; no significant injuries documented from this period beyond the emotional. Relevant medically only in that she is depicted as somatically comfortable with another costumed peer — the same configuration that worked with Peter at his most masked.

**Aguirre-Sacasa *Sensational* and Waid *Daredevil* arcs.** Continued professional work, continued attrition, no novel pathology.

**The Otto/Superior Spider-Man incident — SSM #20 (Slott, 2013).** Catastrophic. Otto-Octavius-occupying-Peter-Parker engages her in combat, uses Spider-Man's strength without Peter's restraint, and beats her in a manner that includes — at minimum — a broken jaw (strongly implied, depicted recovery period consistent), facial lacerations requiring sutures, probable orbital and zygomatic involvement, and unconsciousness on the scene. This is the worst beating depicted in her career. The recovery period extended over months in-narrative.

*Psychological correlate:* the beating was delivered by the man she trusted as her partner-equivalent, in the costume of that partner, with the face of that partner. Every protective frame she had constructed — the mask is the truth, the partner is the safe-because-distant other, my body is the body that cannot be overpowered — was violated simultaneously. This is the closest in-canon analog to the original index trauma: an intimate-coded attacker, physical overpowering, no recourse. Her response — pivot to organized crime, assemble a gang, attempt to kill Spider-Man (ASM vol. 3 #1, #4–5 et seq.) — is consistent with severe PTSD decompensation in a previously compensated survivor under perfect-storm re-traumatization. The medical event is inseparable from the psychiatric event.

**Spencer-era de-escalation.** Gradual return to baseline functioning, partial reconciliation with Peter, return to the playful-thief affect. The somatic recovery preceded the psychiatric recovery by roughly a year of in-story time.

**MacKay solo era (2019–2021).** Several significant operational injuries during the Thieves Guild arcs and the Knull/*King in Black* tie-in (during which she is symbiote-augmented briefly — see Section 6). Cumulative load remains manageable; she is depicted using ice, compression, and an unspecified high-end recovery regimen in her apartment (no medical professional present). The crew (Bruno, Korpse) appears to function as ad-hoc medical support; Doctor Korpse's medical credentials are dubious but operationally sufficient.

**Wells "Heist" era and after.** Continued attrition; no novel pathology of note.

---

### 6. TRANSFORMATIONS AND TEMPORARY AUGMENTATIONS

**Symbiote bonding (*King in Black* tie-in, MacKay run).** Brief bonding with a symbiote during the Knull crisis. Tolerated without depicted long-term sequelae; bond dissolved cleanly. Medically notable as a successful host-symbiote match — she is one of the host candidates whose psychology proved compatible (the symbiote did not find her self-loathing exploitable in the way Eddie Brock's was, because her self-presentation is performatively confident and her actual wounds are sealed under operational identity). The bond left no depicted residual; psychologically she treated the episode as one more costume.

**Magical and probabilistic augmentations across various arcs.** Multiple short-duration enhancements via stolen artifacts in the MacKay run; each treated as a tool, used once, set aside. No long-term integration.

**Notably absent.** No mutate, mutagen, gamma, cosmic, or genetic-engineering exposure in her file. She is, with the singular exception of the Kingpin procedure, somatically baseline human. This is the central medical fact about her: she does what she does in a body that started ordinary.

---

### 7. GYNECOLOGICAL AND SEXUAL HEALTH

No depicted pregnancies. No depicted abortions or miscarriages. No depicted sexually transmitted infections. No depicted contraceptive method, though sexual activity is recurrent across decades — contraception is presumed and unmentioned, consistent with mainstream-comics convention but also with her operational personality, which would not tolerate uncontrolled biological consequence.

Sexual activity is consistently *initiator-controlled*: she opens, she sets pace, she closes. She is not depicted in the receptive-passive posture in any era. This is direct counter-programming against the index trauma's somatic memory. The cost is that genuine surrender — the somatic vulnerability of being received rather than receiving — is essentially absent from her sexual life, which she experiences as freedom and which is also a kind of unhealed scar.

Menstrual function never depicted (genre convention); presumed regular given general somatic regulation. No depicted perimenopausal symptoms in current-era appearances; her biological age in floating-timeline canon places her in the mid-thirties operationally.

No documented history of seeking gynecological care, which — like the absence of any treating physician — reflects both her general avoidance of the medical system and her preference for managing her body privately.

---

### 8. SUBSTANCE USE

**Alcohol.** Light to moderate social use. Champagne in seduction contexts; whiskey in decompression contexts; wine with meals. No depicted intoxication of operational consequence. No pattern consistent with dependence. Alcohol functions as scene-setting and as a controlled lowering of her own guard in carefully chosen settings — it is part of the staging, not a coping mechanism.

**Tobacco.** Not depicted. Inconsistent with the cardiovascular demand of her work.

**Cannabis and other recreational substances.** Not depicted. Inferentially absent — she will not yield cognitive precision to a substance.

**Stimulants and operational aids.** Not depicted. Caffeine presumed. No indication of amphetamine, modafinil, or other performance-pharmaceutical use, which is biographically interesting — many operators in her line use them; she does not, because she has organized her entire identity around the sufficiency of her unaided body.

**Prescription history.** None on file. No depicted use of analgesics beyond presumed over-the-counter post-injury. No psychiatric medication ever depicted or referenced — she has never, in forty-plus years of canon, taken an antidepressant, anxiolytic, or sleep aid. This is consistent with her refusal of the medical system generally and with the specific shame-marker around accepting external augmentation (Section 4).

**Behavioral substitutes.** Risk-seeking is her primary dopaminergic regulator. Heists, rooftop traverses, sexualized confrontation with dangerous men — these provide the neurochemical surge that others derive from drugs. This is a behavioral addiction profile in the technical sense: the activity is over-determined relative to its instrumental purpose, withdrawal produces dysphoria (the bored-Felicia affect in arcs where she is forced to lie low), and the activity is pursued at escalating risk. She would meet criteria for behavioral process addiction if such criteria were formally extended; she does not meet criteria for any chemical-substance disorder.

---

### 9. SLEEP, APPETITE, METABOLIC

**Sleep.** Atypical schedule (operational nights, recovery days), no depicted disturbance of architecture or duration when conditions permit. No depicted parasomnia, no depicted nightmare disorder despite the trauma history — which is either evidence of compensation, evidence of off-panel symptomatology, or both. Her apartment in the MacKay run is depicted as carefully optimized for sleep (heavy curtains, controlled temperature, a bed disproportionate to the room) — the environment of someone who treats sleep as a discipline.

**Appetite.** Normal. Eats well — she enjoys food, is depicted dining out, cooks occasionally (MacKay run). No depicted disordered eating despite the strong cultural pressure on a woman in her presentational mode. Body composition maintained by training load, not restriction.

**Metabolic and cardiovascular.** Implied excellent. Recovery rates and combat endurance imply VO2max in the high range for her body type, resting heart rate likely in the low 50s, blood pressure normal. No depicted endocrine issue.

**Pain tolerance.** High, both constitutionally and through conditioning. Consistent with the "do not be seen recovering" rule.

---

### 10. SYNTHESIS — THE MEDICAL FILE AS PSYCHOLOGICAL DOCUMENT

The medical history reads as a single coherent argument the body has been making for two and a half decades of in-narrative time: *I will not be the body that was violated again, and I will not enter any system — medical, romantic, institutional — that could violate me by knowing me.* The complete absence of a treating physician, the refusal of psychiatric medication, the suspicion of augmentation, the off-panel recoveries, the controlled sexual posture, the disciplined sleep, the disciplined eating, the elite trained capability — these are not separate facts. They are the same fact in different registers.

The two breaches of this argument are the most important entries in the file. The Kingpin's procedure was a breach she invited and concealed and was shamed by; it taught her that augmentation costs. The Otto beating was a breach delivered against her consent by a partner-coded figure; it taught her that the construction is not unbreakable. Both events generated her two worst psychiatric episodes (the post-luck-reveal collapse with Peter; the post-Superior organized-crime arc), and both events were recovered from incompletely — the somatic memory of each persists in specific avoidances and specific rages that are predictable triggers in any future engagement.

The medical prognosis, properly weighted, is *good with caveats*: she is constitutionally robust, behaviorally disciplined, well-conditioned, and has demonstrated capacity to recover from severe injury and severe destabilization. The caveats are (a) the cumulative concussive load is real and unaddressed, (b) the trauma-organized identity has no exit strategy and no provision for a body that ages out of operational capability, and (c) she has no medical or therapeutic relationship to fall back on when the body she has trusted begins, as bodies do, to become a different body.

She has, in essence, built a magnificent house with no door to the outside. The medical file is the floor plan.


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU DOSSIER — FELICIA HARDY
## Section: SOMATIC ATLAS

A total-surveillance file does not merely note that the subject is athletic; it records *how* the athleticism inhabits her at rest, how the body she rebuilt at nineteen carries itself through a grocery aisle at thirty-five, what her face does in the half-second before she lies. What follows is the granular record.

---

### 1. Baseline Architecture

**Build.** Tall (file estimate 5'10"), long-limbed, low body-fat percentage typical of elite gymnasts who have aged into adult musculature — the lat-to-waist ratio of someone who trains pulling movements daily, the shoulder development of years of bar work, the quadriceps and gluteal development of jumping athletes. Hands are working hands beneath the manicure: calloused along the second knuckle of both index fingers (rope and bar), a faint thickening at the ulnar edge of the right palm (knife-hand strikes), short-cut nails on the right hand only — left nails kept slightly longer, an old burglar's tell for tactile work on tumblers and seams.

**Skeletal small data.** Demonstrated history of multiple healed fractures: a left zygomatic-mandibular complex injury consistent with the post-*Superior* assault (faintly asymmetric jawline visible only in three-quarter light), at least one healed metacarpal on the right hand, a left scaphoid that aches in damp weather and is the reason she rotates the left wrist in a slow circle when standing still — a tic she does not know she has. Old hairline rib injuries that produce a barely-detectable favoring of the right side when she laughs hard.

**Skin.** Pale, with the slightly translucent quality that does not tan well; freckles across the bridge of the nose and shoulders, suppressed under makeup in formal mode. Two scars worth note: a thin pale arc below the left ribcage (knife, mid-twenties, undisclosed engagement), and small ladder-pattern scars across the outside of the left thigh consistent with a low-pen graze from her early years, before she trusted her mobility. Both kept off the file in any setting she controls.

**Hair.** Naturally medium brunette; chemically maintained platinum-to-white as adult signature, low-maintenance cut that survives rooftop air, treated weekly. Off-duty: tied back, often with a pencil or a lockpick; she has been observed using both. On-duty civilian: deliberately tousled in a way that takes twenty minutes. In costume context: loose, weaponized — she uses the screen of her own hair to break sightlines on her face.

**Eyes.** Green, large, with a learned wide-eyed default that reads as openness and is in fact a scan posture (peripheral acquisition is improved by a wider palpebral aperture). Pupils run slightly dilated in low-stim conversation — a habit, not a drug sign — which is part of why she registers as flirtatious to interlocutors who don't know they are being surveyed.

---

### 2. Gait, Posture, Locomotion

**Standing baseline.** Weight shifted onto the right leg about sixty percent of the time when at rest, left knee soft, left hand free. This is a gymnast's stage stance carried into civilian life: she is always halfway into a step. Shoulders set markedly back and low — not the rigid carriage of military training but the long-spine carriage of bar work. Chin neutral to slightly elevated. She does not slouch even when alone; her body in private looks like her body in public, which is itself diagnostic — there is no relaxed civilian version to drop into.

**Walk.** Heel-to-toe with notably quiet foot-strike; even in heels she has trained the audible component out. Stride is long for her height, hip-led rather than knee-led, with a subtle counter-rotation through the thoracic spine that reads as sway and is in fact rotational athleticism. She covers ground faster than people expect and adjusts her pace downward to match companions — a courtesy she extends consciously.

**Threat-mode gait.** Shortens stride by roughly fifteen percent, lowers the center of mass two to three inches by softening the knees, brings the hands out of pockets and lets them swing nearer the centerline. Foot-strike becomes ball-first. She looks the same height to a casual observer; she is in fact a different machine.

**Stairs.** Descends two at a time when alone, one at a time and railing-touching when accompanied — performative slowness. Ascends always on the balls of the feet.

**Rooftop and vertical work.** Hand placement is the tell of a trained climber: thumbs wrapped, never flagged. She tests holds with a brief two-kilo loading press before committing. When jumping, she exhales sharply on takeoff (a habit gymnasts and Olympic lifters share) and lands with a quiet double-tap rather than a single thud — front foot, then rear, dispersing impact across two micro-moments.

**Sitting.** Cross-legged at the knee in skirts; cross-legged at the ankle in trousers; rarely uses chair backs — the spine is self-supporting. In booths and on couches she takes the corner seat, back to a wall, sightline to the door. Has done this so long that she is unaware of doing it and will quietly migrate if seated wrong.

---

### 3. Hands and Micro-Manipulation

The hands are the most expressive part of her body and she knows it.

- **Resting hands.** Left hand often at the collarbone or throat, fingers light — a deliberate frame for the face; it reads as flirtation, functions as a vision break that makes her harder to lip-read at distance.
- **Object habit.** Cannot sit with an unattended small object on the table. Coins, lighters, rings, sugar packets, salt cellars, her own earrings if removed — they migrate into her hands and she manipulates them. Coin-rolling across the dorsal knuckles of the right hand is her tonic fidget; she does this in conversations she finds boring, in waiting rooms, on stakeout.
- **Lock-touch.** Walking past any lock, door handle, or latched cabinet, she will trail two fingertips across the mechanism. Half-conscious assessment, half ritual. She does this in friends' homes and is not aware she does it.
- **Eating gestures.** Cutlery held precisely, European style, knife never set down through a course. Wineglass held at the stem, not the bowl, even when drunk.
- **Pocketing.** When she palms a small item — a habit she retains even in legitimate settings — the misdirection is a sweep of hair behind the opposite ear with the empty hand. This tell is consistent enough to function as a signature.

**Stress-state hand pattern.** Under moderate stress the coin-rolling stops; she goes still in the hands. Under acute stress she will tuck both hands under her arms or into her own opposing sleeves — a self-contained, self-soothing posture borrowed from no one. Under threat the hands come up empty and forward at hip height, palms vertical, fingers loose: a fighting-ready frame disguised as conversational gesture.

---

### 4. Face and Micro-Expression

**Default face.** A half-smile carried at low tension on the left side; the right side of the mouth is the genuine one and lifts only when she is actually amused. Photographers and competent interrogators will note that the left-only smile precedes most of her lies and almost all of her seductions.

**Eyebrow.** Single (right) brow lift is her conversational punctuation — interrogative, skeptical, invitational depending on which lip-corner accompanies. The left brow lifts only under genuine surprise, which is rare; cataloguers should treat any independent left-brow event as high-confidence emotional data.

**Eye contact.** Holds it longer than civilians find comfortable, then breaks downward and to her own left — a learned seduction beat. Genuine eye-contact-breaks under emotional pressure go *up* and to her right, a different motion entirely, and are diagnostic.

**Blink rate.** Lower than population baseline in conversation (assess: ~10–12/min) — contributes to the "predator" affect peers describe. Rises sharply (>25/min) during forced unmasking events or when sentimentality from a partner has caught her off guard.

**Lying tells.** Minimal and well-trained. The most reliable: a brief swallow before the sentence, followed by a slightly *over*-relaxed mouth. She does not look away when lying; she over-engages. The tongue-tip touches the upper lip once, fast, before the harder lies. Almost no one catches it.

**Genuine emotional leak points.** The platysma — the broad sheet at the front of the throat — engages microscopically when she is suppressing tears; visible as a vertical tightening below the jaw. The bridge of the nose flushes pink before the cheeks do under shame. Both are sub-second and both are catalogued.

**Laugh.** Two registers. The performed laugh is bell-clear, head tipped back, three to four beats, ends on a downward sigh. The real laugh is lower, almost a chuckle in the chest, eyes crinkle to actual crow's feet, and is accompanied by a quick hand-to-mouth gesture — a vestigial concealment she has never broken.

---

### 5. Voice and Speech Architecture

**Vocal baseline.** Mid-alto, well-supported from the diaphragm, with a trained breath economy — she can speak through a full thirty-second exhale without audible strain. Standard American accent with occasional very faint New York vowels that surface when she is genuinely angry or genuinely tired.

**Cadence.** Conversational tempo is unhurried; she leaves longer pauses than her interlocutors and uses them as instruments. Sentence-final intonation usually downward, declarative, even when the content is a question — a control move. Upspeak appears only in the seduction script and is artificial.

**Volume.** Lower than expected from her physical presence. Forces the listener to lean in. This is calculated and has been calculated since her early twenties.

**Speech under stress.** Tempo *slows*, does not accelerate — the opposite of most people. The quips lengthen. Diction crisps. This is a tell: when Felicia Hardy starts enunciating, the situation has become serious.

**Speech under acute threat or genuine rage.** Drops nearly an octave, loses the music, becomes flat and efficient. Cursing increases. Sentence length shortens to five-to-eight words.

**Self-talk.** Subvocalizes when working a lock or planning a route — small lip movements, no audible sound. Refers to herself in second person ("come on, Cat") during operational stress, third person ("the Cat doesn't —") in jocular off-duty mode, first person only in genuine emotional disclosure, which is rare enough to flag.

---

### 6. Grooming, Adornment, Self-Presentation

**Hygiene cadence.** Showers twice daily as a rule — morning, post-operation or pre-evening. The post-op shower is long (>20 min) and is the closest thing she has to a decompression ritual; observers should treat unusually long showers as affect-processing events.

**Skincare.** Disciplined, multi-step, expensive. The ritual is meditative and protected — she will reschedule meetings rather than skip it.

**Makeup.** Minimal in daylight (concealer, brow, a neutral lip). Maximal at night — winged liner executed without a guide, a signature deep red or wine lip for events she expects to control. The eyeliner is itself a tell: thicker on her left wing than her right by perhaps a millimeter, consistent over years — she paints toward her dominant hand.

**Scent.** A single base perfume worn for over a decade (an oriental-floral with leather notes, file estimate); switches to unscented entirely for operations. Anyone who smells her perfume on an op is being shown it on purpose.

**Wardrobe.** Civilian: tailored to within a centimeter, neutral palette with one statement piece per outfit, almost always a coat or jacket she can move freely in. No restrictive footwear when she has a choice; the heels she does wear are structurally sound enough to fight in and she has. Jewelry: minimal, almost always something she stole, kept for the memory of the steal rather than the object.

**The costume.** Treated as equipment, not as costume — maintained, repaired, inventoried. She suits up in the same order every time: legs, torso, gloves, mask. The mask goes on last and she exhales when it seats. Observers note the exhale; it is the closest thing in her file to a religious gesture.

---

### 7. Sleep Architecture

**Duration.** Five to six hours on operational stretches; seven to eight when stable; will pull a full ten on the first day of decompression and then resume normal. No insomnia per se — she sleeps when she decides to.

**Onset.** Falls asleep in under ten minutes when alone in a known-secure space. With a partner in bed, takes substantially longer; she is incapable of fully letting down with another body present, and partners have reported her appearing asleep for an hour before her breathing actually changes.

**Position.** Sleeps on her left side, right hand under the pillow (knife or pick within reach for most of her adult life — a habit predating real need, and persistent past it). Face toward the room's entry point. If the bed orientation makes this impossible, she will sleep poorly and not know why.

**Architecture.** Light sleeper through the first cycle, deeper through the third and fourth; wakes fully and instantly at unfamiliar sound, with the eyes opening before any other movement — she has trained out the startle flinch. The body stays still while she assesses; this is observable as a held breath of one to three seconds on waking.

**Dream content.** Under-disclosed in canon, but episodes of waking abruptly and showering immediately are documented behaviorally and are the somatic marker of intrusive memory she will not name.

---

### 8. Eating and Appetite

**Pattern.** Two real meals a day, frequent small protein-and-fat snacks (nuts, cheese, charcuterie kept in the kitchen). High caloric ceiling — she trains and recovers. Eats slowly and watches the room while eating; will set down utensils to talk and pick them up again, which paces the meal and conceals appetite.

**Preferences.** Genuine aesthete around food: prefers excellent simple ingredients over elaborate constructions, will spend on wine, knows knives, can actually cook. Coffee is a fixed morning ritual — single-origin, black, no concession.

**Stress eating.** Loses appetite under stress rather than gaining it; will subsist on coffee and protein bars through an operational window and re-feed afterward with a single very good meal taken alone or with crew.

**Drinking.** Functional capacity well above average for body mass — trained tolerance, not biological. Holds three glasses of wine without measurable behavioral change; the fourth produces minor warmth in the cheeks and a slight Brooklyn vowel; she rarely passes that point in company. When she does drink to genuine intoxication, she gets quieter, not louder, and she goes home alone.

---

### 9. Sexual and Intimate Somatics

**Approach posture.** Initiates. Crosses the distance, makes the choice visible, frames the encounter. The body language is forward-weighted hips, hand to the partner's chest or jaw, eye contact held into the kiss. The frame is structurally hers.

**Receptivity.** Performs receptivity convincingly, rarely inhabits it. Partners with sufficient observation report that she remains essentially the actor in the scene — coordinating, pacing, watching — and that the moments she actually surrenders are vanishingly rare and unmistakable when they happen (the breath drops, the eyes close fully, the hands go slack rather than gripping).

**After.** Does not linger. Up within twenty minutes, hydration, shower, either return to bed in a controlled cuddle posture (her back to him, his arm where she can move it) or full departure. Sleep-overs at a partner's residence are rare and reserved for relationships she has formally categorized as safe.

**Withdrawal cues.** When intimacy threatens her frame she becomes *more* sexual, not less — escalates the physical to derail the emotional. Cataloguers should read sudden increases in seductive tempo during emotionally exposing conversations as defensive maneuvers, not as desire.

**Touch tolerance, non-sexual.** Surprisingly low with strangers and acquaintances; high with the small inner circle. Will not be touched on the lower back or the back of the neck by anyone she has not consented to be touched there by — vestigial vigilance from the index trauma. Hand on her wrist from behind is the single most reliably destabilizing non-violent touch in her file.

---

### 10. State-Dependent Modulation: A Summary

**Calm (baseline, secure, in-circle).** Posture loose-tall, coin rolling, real laugh present, hair tied back, left brow available, hands free with objects, voice mid-alto with longer pauses, eats normally, sleeps deep, will tolerate touch from intimates.

**Mild stress (operation in planning, hostile social).** Hands still, weight more evenly distributed, left-only smile dominant, eyeline scan expands, blink rate steady-low, speech tempo slows by perhaps ten percent, dressing becomes more deliberate.

**Acute stress (operation live, ethically loaded encounter).** Center of mass drops, foot-strike becomes ball-first, hands forward at hip height, voice quieter and crisper, eye contact tighter, breath economy lengthens, appetite gone, peripheral vision actively used, micro-expressions suppressed almost entirely.

**Threat (overpowering male presence, physical engagement).** Voice drops register and loses music, cursing rises, breathing through the nose, posture sets into a fighting frame disguised as casual stance, peripheral object inventory continuous (anything in the room that can become a weapon is logged within seconds), pain response notably blunted.

**Intimate exposure (a partner naming something true).** Platysma engages, nose-bridge flushes, blink rate spikes, eye-break upward-right, body leans toward escape vector while voice stays light — and within thirty seconds either a quip arrives or a hand goes to the partner's body to redirect the moment back into the physical register. The whole sequence is two breaths long and almost no one sees it.

**Wounded state (post-humiliation, post-betrayal).** All performance drops; the body goes economic and silent, hands inside opposing sleeves, sits low and against a wall, will eat nothing for a day, will not be touched, will refuse company except — historically — one trusted figure at a time. The recovery vector is consistent: presence without demand, in a safe room, with the lights low. Given that, the body reorganizes inside forty-eight hours. Denied it, she will instead reorganize *outward* into the colder, predatory operational mode the file documents under maximum-injury conditions, and the somatic markers of that mode — flat voice, dead eyes, economical violence — should be treated as the single most reliable warning sign in her entire profile.

---

*End Section. Cross-reference: Section 3 (Psychological — defenses and affect regulation), Section 4 (Psychiatric — decompensation triggers), and forthcoming Section on Operational Tradecraft.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — FELICIA HARDY (BLACK CAT)
## Section: Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### I. Attachment Classification and Etiology

The subject's attachment organization is best characterized as **dismissive-avoidant with a concealed anxious-preoccupied substrate** — what the Adult Attachment literature would call a *fearful-avoidant* presentation that has stabilized over decades into a high-functioning dismissive surface. The fearful core is rarely visible; the dismissive shell is on continuous display. Distinguishing the two matters operationally: a true dismissive does not pursue. Felicia pursues. She pursues theatrically, repeatedly, across forty years of canon, while disclaiming the pursuit and structuring it so that the pursued object can never quite close the distance. This is not indifference to attachment; it is **attachment routed through a containment system**.

Etiology resolves into three developmental insults stacked across roughly fifteen years of her early life:

**1. The idealized-absent father (childhood through adolescence).** Walter Hardy was, by Felicia's own account and the available canon, present as iconography and absent as parent. His criminal career produced a household organized around mystique, secrecy, and the periodic disappearance of the primary male attachment figure. The internal working model laid down in this period: *the man I love is the man who is not here, and the man who is not here is the man I love.* This is not metaphor; it is the literal template she would later operationalize with every masked partner she chose. The first thing she did upon learning the truth of his identity was not to confront him, not to grieve, but to **become him** — Black Cat is, at the iconographic level, a costume designed to extend Walter's brand. Identification-with-the-absent-object is among the most stable defenses against attachment loss, and it pre-dates her trauma.

**2. The sexual assault by Ryan (Empire State, freshman year).** The violation occurred during the developmental window in which her first adult attachment was forming — exactly the moment at which the dating-and-mating system was being calibrated. The result is a permanent cross-wiring of the attachment, sexual, and threat systems. In ordinary development these systems share circuitry but remain functionally distinct; in Felicia's case, sexual desire, attachment longing, and threat-vigilance fire together. This explains, with no further hypothesis required, why she eroticizes danger, why she selects partners who are literal physical threats, and why she experiences ordinary tender intimacy as flat or even mildly aversive — it is missing the threat valence the system was tuned to require.

**3. The pre-empted revenge (the discovery of Ryan's death).** The energy mobilized to kill her rapist had no terminal object. This is the most under-appreciated trauma in her file. A completed revenge — even a refused revenge — would have given the system an endpoint. The drunk-driving death denied her catharsis and left a permanently energized retaliatory circuit with no target. That circuit *had* to find expression, and it found it in two displacements: (a) the costume and the career, which give the rage a daily occupation; and (b) the partnered relationship, in which the male other is repeatedly tested — *can you overpower me? will you? what happens if you do?* — and rewarded with intimacy if the test is passed without violation.

The compound result: a woman who needs closeness, cannot tolerate being known, requires that her partner be powerful enough to hurt her, requires that he refuse to, and requires that this be re-tested perpetually.

---

### II. The Bonding Sequence — Granular Choreography

Across canon, Felicia's bonding behaviors follow a stereotyped six-phase sequence so consistent that it functions as a behavioral fingerprint.

**Phase 1 — Acquisition.** She selects the target, almost always against operational logic. The target is a man who is (a) masked or otherwise structurally unavailable, (b) demonstrably her physical equal or superior, (c) ethically constrained in a way that prevents him from using his power against her, and (d) already entangled with another woman or another life. Spider-Man, the Foreigner, Daredevil, briefly Flash, and the rotating roster around the Thieves Guild all satisfy at least three of four. She does not select available men. When an available man is offered (the civilian Peter, repeatedly), she experiences a marked drop in interest that she herself does not fully understand and rationalizes as the man being "boring."

**Phase 2 — Theatrical approach.** First contact is staged. She arranges the meeting — usually on or adjacent to a heist — so that the encounter occurs on her chosen terrain, at her chosen tempo, with her in costume and the target reacting. The crime *is* the introduction. This serves three functions: it confirms her competence to the target before he has a chance to underestimate her; it places the interaction in a register (play, danger, performance) she controls; and it externalizes the affect, allowing her to display arousal as professional excitement rather than personal want.

**Phase 3 — Calibrated escalation.** She tests across several axes in rapid sequence — physical (can he keep up), ethical (will he draw a line, where), tactical (does he read her), and erotic (does he respond to flirtation, and how). The data from these tests are integrated quickly. She is unusually skilled at reading partners; the relational impulsivity noted in the psychological section coexists with extraordinary tactical perception within a single encounter. A partner who fails the ethical test — uses excessive force, threatens a civilian, attempts to coerce her — is dropped instantly and without grief. A partner who passes is moved to Phase 4.

**Phase 4 — Sexualization on her initiative.** The first physical intimacy is invariably initiated by her, on terrain she chose, at a moment she selected. She does not allow the other party to set the tempo of the first physical encounter. This is over-determined: it is partly seduction-as-craft, partly assertion that this body is hers to deploy, and partly a literal reversal of the rape — *I decide when, where, who, how*. Note that this is **not** a performance for the partner's benefit; it is a regulatory operation for her own nervous system. The partner is the occasion.

**Phase 5 — The plateau.** A period — sometimes weeks of canon-time, sometimes years — during which she maintains the relationship at a steady distance. Affection is real; commitment is structurally precluded. She lives parallel to the partner rather than entangled with him. Cohabitation is rare and short-lived; logistical interdependence is avoided; she keeps her own safehouses, her own crew, her own income streams. The plateau can be remarkably stable for an avoidant attachment, and this is one of the file's interesting features: when the partner respects the distance, the relationship can persist for extended periods at a real and warm level.

**Phase 6 — The exit, or the cycle.** Termination is triggered by one of three events: (a) the partner demands more proximity than the plateau permits (Peter's repeated bids for unmasked civilian intimacy), (b) the partner discovers something concealed (the luck-powers reveal, ASM #289 era), or (c) an external shock destabilizes her enough that she cannot maintain the plateau and chooses to break it preemptively rather than be seen breaking. Exits are characteristically *clean on the surface and unresolved underneath*. She does not stage breakup dramas; she withdraws, often via a quip, and reconfigures her life around the loss within days. The lack of mourning behavior is itself the mourning — the affect goes underground and emerges weeks or months later as a rebound choice (the Foreigner after Peter; the Thieves Guild entanglements after subsequent losses).

The cycle, critically, is *re-enterable*. She returns to former partners. The plateau can be re-established. She does not bridge-burn except under extreme injury (the Otto incident, which was not Peter's fault but registered as a Peter-failure regardless).

---

### III. Distrust Architecture

Distrust in this subject is **not** a presenting affect; it is a structural feature so deeply built into the operating system that she rarely notices it. She does not feel suspicious; she simply behaves as if betrayal is the default expected outcome and is mildly surprised when it does not occur.

Observable distrust behaviors, longitudinal:

- **Compartmentalization of information.** No partner is ever given the full picture. Peter never knew the luck-powers origin until forced disclosure. Crew members in the MacKay era are given operational need-to-know only. Former partners are rarely told why she left.
- **Concealment of vulnerability states.** Injury, fatigue, fear, and grief are systematically hidden. The quip is the primary tool. When the body itself betrays her (the Otto-era beating) she withdraws from contact rather than allow herself to be seen weak.
- **Pre-emptive infidelity-of-frame.** She often introduces a third party (another flirtation, another job, another safehouse) into the relational field as an insurance policy against being the one who is left. This is not promiscuity per se; it is a structural hedge.
- **Surveillance of partners.** Implicit across canon — she *knows* where her partners are, who they are with, what they are doing — partly tradecraft, partly attachment-vigilance dressed as tradecraft.
- **Asymmetry of disclosure.** She extracts more information from partners than she gives. This is so habitual that she likely does not register it as imbalance.

Trust is extended in a counter-intuitive pattern: **operationally fast, emotionally glacial**. She will let a near-stranger have her back in a firefight long before she will let a years-long partner see her cry. Operational trust costs her little (she can survive operational betrayal); emotional trust is rationed because the index trauma was an emotional trust that became a physical violation. The lesson the body learned at nineteen was that the man who is permitted into intimate proximity is the man who can do the unsurvivable thing. The system has not been re-trained because no relationship has been allowed to last long enough at sufficient depth to re-train it.

---

### IV. Betrayal — Done To Her and Done By Her

**Done to her.** The catalogue is dense. Ryan, foundationally. The Kingpin's people, who exploited her insecurity to install the luck-field and own her by proxy. Peter, repeatedly, for the crime of being a different person than the man she had bonded with — and again, in her framing, for the crime of marrying Mary Jane. The Foreigner. Otto-as-Peter, who delivered the most acute somatic betrayal of the modern era and who she experienced as Peter regardless of the metaphysics. Each betrayal was metabolized via the same protocol: short interval of cold rage, decisive operational pivot, no expressed grief. The Otto incident is the cleanest case study — the response was not to mourn Peter or to seek understanding but to assemble a gang and attempt his execution. Betrayal, in her schema, is an event that demands a counter-move, not an event that demands processing.

**Done by her.** Felicia betrays partners with a specific and limited grammar. She does not betray operationally — her crew is safe, her allies' lives are protected, her word in the field is good. She betrays **at the level of disclosure and presence**. She withholds. She leaves. She lets a partner believe a thing she has not corrected. She conceals the luck-powers. She conceals the depth of her feeling for Peter from Peter, and conceals the depth of her feeling for other partners from herself. She is capable of using sex instrumentally and has done so (the Foreigner arc is the clearest depicted instance). She will, under sufficient narcissistic injury, weaponize intimate knowledge — though notably, even in the post-Superior heat, she did not expose Peter's identity, which is data: there is a floor below which she does not go.

The asymmetry is diagnostic. She experiences others' betrayals as catastrophic frame-violations requiring retaliation; she experiences her own betrayals as legitimate self-protection requiring no defense. This is the predictable cognitive distortion of the trauma-organized attachment system, and she is not unusual in displaying it.

---

### V. Repair — Capacity, Conditions, Limits

Repair in this subject is **real, slow, and conditional**. She is capable of it, which distinguishes her from the Cluster B presentations the surface suggests. The conditions are stringent.

Repair requires:

1. **Time and distance first.** She cannot repair in the heat. Attempting to address rupture in the immediate aftermath produces sharper withdrawal. The interval is usually weeks to months.
2. **The other party making the first re-approach** — but doing so without demanding accountability. If the re-approach is framed as "you owe me an apology," she will refuse and the breach widens. If the re-approach is framed as presence offered without condition, she will often accept.
3. **An indirect channel for the apology.** She apologizes via action, gift, or favor, rarely via words. A successfully completed joint operation can serve as the entire reconciliation. The verbal apology, when it occurs, is brief, dry, and immediately deflected with humor.
4. **No revisiting.** Once a repair is achieved, the rupture is not to be discussed again. Attempts to "process" the prior breach are experienced as fresh attacks.
5. **The other party demonstrating that they have not used the breach to learn weaponizable things about her.** This is critical and easy to miss: she watches, after a repair, for evidence that the partner has filed away the wound for later use. If she detects this, the repair reverses irreversibly.

Within these limits, the repairs she has executed (with Peter across multiple cycles, with the Black Fox, with members of her crew, with various peripheral allies) are durable. She does not perform repair; when she has done it, she has done it.

---

### VI. Intimacy and Dependency — The Plateau Architecture

The single most stable feature of her intimate life is the **plateau** — the maintained mid-distance at which she is most functional and most herself. Imagine a relational dial with three settings: stranger, plateau, fused. She lives almost exclusively at plateau. Fused terrifies her; stranger bores her. The plateau permits desire, banter, mutual aid, periodic sex, real affection, and the experience of being chosen, without exposing her to the conditions under which the index trauma occurred (a partner with intimate knowledge and unchecked access).

Dependency, in the ordinary sense, is **absent**. She does not lean. She does not call for help. She does not require logistical interdependence. She earns her own money, maintains her own residences, makes her own meals, schedules her own life. The few visible instances of her accepting help (Doctor Strange removing the luck-field; her crew supporting her in the MacKay era) are exceptions that prove the rule and are accepted only when the alternative is operational failure.

What she does require, beneath the avoidant surface, is **witness**. She wants to be seen — by someone competent, by someone who will not look away, by someone who will register the craft and the cost of who she has become. This is the anxious substrate under the dismissive shell. It is why she selects partners who are themselves heroes-in-masks: only such a partner is positioned to witness her without being able to coerce her. The witnessing relationship — Peter, at his best — is the closest she gets to dependency, and even that she rations.

Sexually, the dependency pattern repeats: she is the initiator, the framer, the one who decides the encounter is over. She does not appear to permit herself the receptive, surrendered posture that would replicate the somatic conditions of the assault. Whether she can has not been depicted; the operating presumption of the file is that she has not allowed it and would experience attempts to invite it as threats.

---

### VII. The Template — The One Relationship She Has, Over and Over

Beneath every named partner is the same relational structure, repeated with variations:

> *A powerful, ethically-constrained, structurally-unavailable man encounters her in a context of mutual risk. She tests him. He passes. They circle. She initiates physically. They establish a plateau. He eventually wants more. She withdraws — sometimes cleanly, sometimes via a third-party complication, sometimes via a concealed truth coming out. They separate. Time passes. They re-encounter. The plateau is re-established at a slightly different angle. Repeat.*

Every significant relationship in the canon is a variation on this template. Spider-Man is the purest case and the one against which she calibrates. The Foreigner inverted the ethics axis (a man she could not trust morally), and the relationship ran shorter and colder. Daredevil offered an interesting variant in which the masked man already had a deeper trauma profile of his own; the encounter was brief and notably non-escalatory because his structure mirrored hers too closely to function as a stable other. The MacKay-era figures (Odessa Drake most notably) extend the template into same-sex flirtation territory, with the same plateau dynamics — proximity, play, mutual respect, no commitment.

The template is the symptom and the solution simultaneously. It is how she keeps having attachment-experiences without permitting the conditions of the index injury to recur. It is also why she has not formed a primary, civilian, committed, exposed relationship in forty years of in-universe time — the template architecturally precludes it.

The two routes by which the template could be revised are visible in the canon. The first is **mentorship of younger thieves**, where she occupies the protector-witness role that would have saved her at nineteen. This appears to be doing genuine repair work; the maternal-protective stance reactivates the attachment system in a low-threat configuration and lets her practice presence-without-flight with people whose dependency on her she can tolerate because she is the one in the powerful position. The second is **a partner willing to live indefinitely at the plateau without escalating** — which, by the structure of heroic narrative, no Peter Parker can sustainably do, because the demand for resolution is built into him. Until or unless she encounters a partner whose own structure prefers the plateau, the template will continue to run.

The synthesis: she is not avoidant of love. She is avoidant of the conditions under which love, at nineteen, became the vehicle of unsurvivable harm. The distinction matters because the path forward — the one the MacKay run gestures at — is not the discovery of a "right partner" who will breach her defenses, but the slow accumulation of evidence, across many partners and many years, that the conditions have changed. She is doing this work. She has been doing it the entire time. The file should be read accordingly.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — FELICIA HARDY (BLACK CAT)
## SECTION: DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

---

### Preamble: The Architecture as a Whole

A defensive system is legible by its *layering* — what the subject reaches for first, what she falls back on under pressure, and what is held in reserve for catastrophic threat. Felicia Hardy's architecture is unusually well-organized for a trauma-formed adult: she has a deep bench of mature defenses (sublimation, humor, altruism) sitting on top of a middle stratum of neurotic-grade operations (reaction formation, intellectualization-as-planning, eroticization), with a thin but real floor of more primitive material (devaluation, mild splitting, acting-out, omnipotent control) that surfaces only under specific provocations — sexual humiliation, forced unmasking, physical domination by a male. The system is *engineered*, not improvised. That is the central observation. Most of the defenses she runs are deployed with awareness; she is not the patient who does not know she is doing it. She is the patient who chose her defenses the way she chose her grappling style.

The ranking that follows moves from most primitive to most mature, with behavioral exemplars from canon for each. The mature end of the spectrum is heavier than the primitive end — which is the prognostic good news in the file.

---

### Stratum I — Primitive Defenses (low frequency, high voltage)

These activate only under acute decompensation. They are not her ordinary mode of being.

**1. Acting-Out.** The clearest exemplar is the post-Superior pivot (ASM vol. 3 #1, #4–5): physically beaten and humiliated by Otto-in-Peter's-body, she does not process the injury; she discharges it by *constructing an enterprise* — assembling a gang, taking territory, pursuing Spider-Man's death. The acting-out is sophisticated (she does not break windows; she builds a criminal organization) but it is acting-out nonetheless — the affect cannot be tolerated and must be converted into externally-directed activity at scale. The recovery from this period is slow precisely because the defense was so structurally elaborated that walking it back required dismantling a literal organization. Smaller-scale acting-out punctuates the long arc whenever a romantic disappointment lands: she rebounds into a heist, into a new partner, into the Foreigner (Web #6) — the body must be in motion or the affect catches up.

**2. Devaluation (rebound-grade).** When exposure occurs — Peter learning about the luck-powers bargain, Peter's marriage, Otto's beating — Felicia swings, sometimes within a single scene, from idealization or affection to contempt. The devaluation is brittle: it does not hold, she returns, she re-engages. This is the diagnostically important detail — borderline-grade devaluation is *stable* in the moment and recurrent; Felicia's is a discharge mechanism that resolves once the humiliation metabolizes. She uses it to put distance between herself and the wound, not to actually annihilate the object.

**3. Mild Splitting (functional, not pathological).** Felicia/Black Cat is not a dissociative split — she is one woman, continuously aware. But there is a *micro-split* in how she treats the same object across role-states: Peter-the-man and Spider-Man-the-mask are processed as if they were different attachment objects, with different rules and different permitted intimacies (ASM #258, #283 are the cleanest demonstrations). She knows they are one person; she behaves as if they are two. The defense is used to permit desire toward an object that civilian-self contact would render unsafe.

**4. Omnipotent Control (situational).** Under maximal threat she reaches for a fantasy of total control over the field — the luck powers were the literal somatic incarnation of this defense (a probability field bending reality around her). The decision to accept the Kingpin's modification (ASM #220s, revealed #245) is the single clearest behavioral signature of omnipotent control as defense: rather than tolerate the experience of being-less-than-Peter in a shared operational field, she altered the universe's odds in her favor. The defense's failure (the luck backwashing onto loved ones) is correspondingly the most chastening event in her adult life and the one most responsible for the partial maturation visible in later eras.

**5. Somatization-Adjacent Counterphobic Compulsion.** Not somatization proper (she does not convert affect into illness), but the body is recruited to bind anxiety — she must train, must move, must put herself in physical danger to discharge what she cannot feel. Under stress, the workout intensifies, the route becomes harder, the heist gets riskier. This is a primitive-end defense because it is *compulsive* rather than chosen; when she cannot move, she degrades.

---

### Stratum II — Neurotic-Grade Defenses (ordinary daily operation)

This is where Felicia mostly lives. These are the defenses doing the heavy daily work.

**6. Reaction Formation.** The single most foundational defense. The raped college freshman becomes the unflappable seductress; the helpless body becomes the elite athlete; the woman who was overpowered becomes the woman who is never not-in-control of a physical encounter. The behavioral signature is the *180-degree quality* — she has not become merely confident, she has become the inverse of what she was made to feel. This is why the persona is theatrical and why the sexuality is performative: reaction formations are always slightly louder than authentic traits, because they are working against the polar opposite. The tell is the over-determined ease — too smooth, too unbothered, in scenes that would unsettle most operators.

**7. Counterphobia.** Adjacent to but distinct from reaction formation. Counterphobia is the active seeking out of the feared situation in order to master it. Felicia's professional life is a continuous counterphobic exposure protocol: she repeatedly puts herself in physically vulnerable positions vis-à-vis powerful, dangerous men (Spider-Man, Daredevil, the Foreigner, Kingpin-orbit figures, the Thieves Guild) and emerges in control. Each successful cycle is a corrective experience to the original trauma — *I went into the room with the dangerous man and this time I left on my terms*. The defense is genuinely therapeutic at low doses; at high doses (the more dangerous the antagonist, the more she escalates) it shades into compulsive reenactment.

**8. Eroticization of Threat.** A specific and characteristic neurotic operation: anxiety attached to a stimulus is converted into desire for that stimulus. The dangerous other becomes the desired other.
