With minimal institutional or familial scaffolding (an incarcerated father, an absent ethical authority during the assault and its aftermath, a profession that does not come with a manual), she has constructed and *maintained* a coherent personal ethics:

- Civilians are off the table. This is enforced internally even when it costs her operationally.
- Targets skew toward the wealthy, the corrupt, the institutionally protected. There is a redistributive intuition under the heist aesthetic, even when she does not articulate it.
- Lethal force is a last resort, not a preferred tool. Across decades the body count attributable to her direct action is conspicuously low for a career criminal at her operational tempo.
- In-group protection is non-negotiable.
- The work should be beautiful. Sloppy crime is bad crime; the aesthetic standard is also an ethical one because it forces planning, which forces care, which lowers collateral harm.

The code is not perfect and she violates it under acute injury (the post-Superior arc being the documented exception). But it exists, it is hers, and it holds across most loads. Self-authored ethics in the absence of institutional scaffolding is, clinically, a stronger indicator of moral development than rule-following inside a structure that compels rules.

**Selective conscience that functions.** She feels shame in the right places (the luck-powers concealment) and does not feel shame in places she has rightly rejected the imposition of it (her sexuality, her profession's victimless dimensions). The calibration is unusual and largely sound.

---

### VI. PROFESSIONAL & MATERIAL CAPITAL

**Financial independence.** She is functionally wealthy, off-books, with the asset distribution discipline of a successful professional criminal — multiple identities, multiple safehouses across at least the New York metro and likely beyond, fenced-asset liquidity, jurisdictional diversification of holdings. She has never been depicted in genuine economic precarity as an adult.

**Reputation as a resource.** The Black Cat name has market value in the criminal underworld and recognition value above it. She has cultivated it consciously: signature, calling card, controlled myth. The Thieves Guild material (MacKay) demonstrates she can convert reputation into structural position when she chooses to.

**Network breadth.** Spans the legitimate (museum and gallery contacts, charity-circuit access), the gray (private security, information brokers, the Foreigner-class operators), and the criminal (Thieves Guild, fences, specialist crews). She maintains the network actively, with the social investment costs paid in advance so that calls are returned when she places them.

**Mentees and inheritors.** The mentorship dimension is a genuine asset, not a vanity. Younger thieves under her wing represent both operational extension and meaning-structure — and the MacKay-era integration shows that the mentor role does for her psychologically what nothing else has quite managed: it gives her a version of the adult-protector figure she did not have at nineteen, by letting her *be* one.

---

### VII. RESILIENCE FACTORS, MECHANISTIC

The catalogue above describes assets. This section describes *why they hold*.

**1. Refunctioning of symptoms into skills.** Hypervigilance became professional situational awareness. Counterphobic risk-seeking became operational competence. The compulsion to control the frame became a coherent interpersonal style that, while limiting in intimacy, is wildly effective in operations and leadership. This is the central resilience mechanism: she does not fight her symptoms, she employs them, and the employment is productive.

**2. Identity that survives setback.** The Felicia/Black Cat construction is criticized elsewhere in the file as a defense, but it is also a *stable* defense, and stability of identity is a primary resilience asset. She knows who she is across decades. She does not fragment under stress; she narrows.

**3. Behavioral substitute for chemical regulation.** She has a non-pharmacological mood regulator that works: the work itself. Heisting, training, planning, executing — these reliably produce the dopaminergic and noradrenergic profile she needs to feel regulated, without the cumulative toxicity of substance dependence. The risk is real (the behavioral-addiction profile is legible), but the trade against alcoholism or opioid dependence is favorable, and her substance-use history is conspicuously clean.

**4. Multiple meaning-sources.** Craft, aesthetics, mentorship, in-group bonds, the long Peter-thread, the long Walter-thread. If any single meaning-source fails she does not collapse; the load redistributes. Survivors with single-pillar meaning structures are far more brittle.

**5. Capacity to learn across the long arc.** The trajectory from the Wolfman/DeFalco-era femme-fatale-foil to the MacKay-era crew leader with an ethos is a real developmental arc, not just a writerly drift. She has metabolized experience and integrated it. The MacKay-era version is more honest, more relationally available within her limits, and more ethically articulated than the 1980s version. Growth is observable.

**6. Selective use of help.** She does not seek formal treatment, but she uses the help she will accept: Peter's moral framing when she needs an anchor, the Black Fox's elder-thief counsel, her crew's affection, occasionally Strange's literal intervention (the luck-field excision). The pattern is restrictive but not absent.

**7. Frame control as protective layer, not only defensive one.** The same control mechanism that limits intimacy also reliably protects her from re-victimization at the operational level. It is a load-bearing structure, and recognizing that it carries protective weight is necessary to understand why she does not simply abandon it.

---

### VIII. LATENT & UNDER-USED CAPACITIES

A complete asset ledger names what is in inventory but not yet deployed at scale.

- **Leadership at organizational scale.** She has run crews; she has not run institutions. The MacKay arc suggests she could, and the Thieves Guild material gestures at it. The capacity is there; the inclination is gated by her preference for the smaller, controllable unit.
- **Teaching.** The mentorship instinct is real and could extend well beyond burglary craft to broader survivorship work, if she ever permitted herself that public-facing role.
- **Civilian competence.** Never seriously tested because never seriously attempted. The cognitive and aesthetic equipment to operate at a high level in legitimate art, security consulting, or gallery curation is fully present.
- **Sustained partnership.** Latent rather than absent. The capacity for it is demonstrated in flashes; the structural permissions are what she has not yet built. The MacKay-era trajectory suggests this is the next frontier rather than a permanent foreclosure.
- **Grief work.** The single largest unprocessed reservoir, and therefore the largest potential gain. The capacity to access it exists — it surfaces briefly in *Evil That Men Do* and again in the Superior aftermath — but it has never been worked through. If it ever were, the energy currently bound to compensation would be substantially liberated.

---

### IX. DURABILITY ASSESSMENT

Against chronic background load: **very high**. She has sustained a double life, professional-tempo operations, and a contested social position for over two decades in-canon without burnout, somatic collapse, or substance escape. Few comparable operators in the file have her endurance profile.

Against acute injury: **moderate, with brittle ceiling**. The compensated structure handles ordinary acute injury well — she absorbs losses, setbacks, and ordinary humiliations within her normal range. Above a specific threshold (sexual humiliation, being physically overpowered by a male antagonist, exposure of concealed shame), the structure collapses to the cold predatory mode. This ceiling is documented; it is also lower than it used to be, suggesting genuine resilience-building over the long arc.

Against structural threat to in-group: **uncharacteristically reckless, but functionally effective**. The recklessness is real and operationally suboptimal, but it has not yet produced catastrophic failure, and the underlying loyalty is itself the asset that generates the in-group capable of protecting her in return.

---

### X. SYNTHESIS

The file should record, plainly, that Felicia Hardy is a *successful* trauma adaptation. The phrase is not an oxymoron. She took the worst night of a nineteen-year-old's life and, with materials no one handed her, built four decades of sustained competence, durable loyalties, a self-authored ethics that mostly holds, a body that still works, a mind that still sharpens, a circle that loves her, and a craft she practices beautifully. The costs are real and have been accounted elsewhere. The assets are also real and have been undercounted. The clinical importance of this ledger is straightforward: any intervention, alliance, or assessment that treats her as primarily a pathology-bearer rather than as a high-functioning survivor with a specific set of unresolved frontiers will misjudge both her capacity and her trajectory. She is, on the evidence, still getting better. The dossier should weight that.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU DOSSIER — FELICIA HARDY (BLACK CAT)
## Section 7: Failure Modes & Decompensation

---

### 7.1 Preliminary: What "Breaking" Means for This Subject

Felicia Hardy does not break the way fragile people break. Her structure is, in fact, unusually robust under most categories of pressure that disable comparable operators — physical injury, financial loss, betrayal by acquaintances, the death of secondary attachments, public exposure of her criminal identity (the public has *always* known about Black Cat; that channel of shame is pre-burned and inert). The compensated PTSD architecture documented in §4 is load-bearing precisely because it was *built* — selected, drilled, and lived-in across the developmental window between nineteen and her mid-twenties. The structure is therefore narrow but deep: she has high resilience along the axes she designed for and almost no resilience along the axes she designed *against*.

Decompensation, when it occurs, is therefore not a generalized collapse. It is a phase transition along one of three predictable failure axes. Each axis has its own escalation curve, its own behavioral signature, its own duration, and its own recovery profile. They can compound — most catastrophically, the Otto sequence in *Superior Spider-Man* #20 hit all three simultaneously — but they fail in characteristic ways and can be tracked independently.

The three axes:

1. **The Humiliation Axis** — sexualized, gendered, or physical overpowering by a male antagonist.
2. **The Exposure Axis** — being *seen* in a way she did not author; the unmasking, literal or psychological, that strips frame control.
3. **The Attachment Axis** — loss, betrayal, or sentimental violation by a primary attachment figure (historically Peter; latterly her crew).

Each is treated below in clinical detail.

---

### 7.2 The Humiliation Axis: Re-Evocation of Index Trauma

#### Trigger profile

The cleanest trigger is a physically dominant male antagonist inflicting bodily damage on her in a manner she cannot frame, narrate, or refuse. The canonical instance is Otto Octavius in Spider-Man's body beating her unconscious and dislocating her jaw (*Superior Spider-Man* #20, 2013). Lesser instances scatter across the file: the Foreigner's enforcers in the late '80s arcs; the Tombstone confrontation in MacKay's run; the Maggia underbosses she handles with a calibrated mixture of contempt and care precisely because the physical-overpowering category is *the* live wire.

The trigger is not "violence." Felicia takes hits constantly without destabilization. The trigger is the *structure* of the violence: male body overpowering hers, with no frame she authored, and a witnessable aftermath. This is the index trauma's somatic signature, and the body recognizes it before cognition does.

#### Escalation curve

- **T+0 to T+hours:** Behavioral mutism in the immediate aftermath. She does not narrate the event, does not quip, does not file the standard ironic distance. The absence of a quip is the *single most diagnostic early sign* this axis has been activated; her baseline is a wisecrack within ninety seconds of any setback, and its absence indicates the verbal-distancing defense has gone offline.
- **T+hours to T+days:** Hyperfocus on physical recovery. Training intensifies. Food intake drops (mild — sub-clinical, but present). Sleep architecture shifts toward shorter, lighter cycles consistent with hypervigilant reset.
- **T+days to T+weeks:** Cognitive reframing toward grievance. She begins constructing a *case* against the perpetrator, but unlike her usual operational planning, the planning is suffused with affect — wider scope, harsher means, less surgical execution. This is when the ethical perimeter (no civilians, non-lethal default) begins to erode at the edges.
- **T+weeks to T+months:** The cold operational mode consolidates. In the Otto sequence, this manifested as the organized-crime pivot — building a crew, taking territory, attempting to kill Spider-Man (*Amazing Spider-Man* vol. 3 #1, #4–5). The grandiosity is structural compensation for the somatic humiliation; she becomes *larger* in the only domain she trusts (operational power) to overwrite the smallness imposed on her body.

#### Behavioral signature in decompensated state

- Speech rate drops 20–30% from baseline; sentences shorten; the trailing playful clause disappears.
- Smile musculature shows recruitment without ocular involvement — the classic non-Duchenne presentation; her baseline Duchenne smile is rare in this state.
- Touch tolerance collapses. Where baseline Felicia initiates and welcomes incidental physical contact (a hand on a shoulder, the arm-loop greeting), in this state proximity within 18 inches produces a micro-recoil and re-positioning, usually disguised as a step toward something operational.
- Sexual behavior bifurcates: either complete withdrawal from the domain, or instrumentalized predation with no genuine arousal signal — a re-mastering enactment that is itself a symptom.
- Recreational reading, gallery visits, the aesthetic intake she normally uses for regulation — drops to near zero. The MacKay-era Felicia is a woman who looks at paintings; the post-Otto Felicia is not.

#### Recovery profile

Recovery on this axis is *slow* (months to a year) and requires the somatic re-mastery loop to close — typically through a confrontation with the perpetrator in which she dictates terms, *or* a substitute confrontation in which she physically dominates a structurally similar antagonist with witnesses she trusts. Talk therapy (or its in-canon equivalent — being listened to by Peter, by the Black Fox, by her crew) cannot complete this loop. The body has to win the fight the body lost.

---

### 7.3 The Exposure Axis: Frame Violation and Unmasking

#### Trigger profile

Any event in which Felicia is *seen* — accurately, in her unmediated state — by a witness she did not authorize. The paradigm instance is the ASM #245 reveal sequence in which Peter learns the Kingpin gave her the luck powers and that she concealed it. The structural element is not the secret itself; it is that *the secret was the frame*, and the frame was the safety. When Peter saw the rigging behind the performance, he saw Felicia in the configuration she most fears: small, bargaining, dependent on a man's regard for her own adequacy.

Other instances:
- Peter unmasking and her visible disappointment (ASM #194 et seq., revisited #258, #283). She experiences the *reverse* of an unmasking — the costume she desired turning out to contain a civilian — as its own frame violation; her object choice depended on the mystery, and she resents its dissolution.
- The "One More Day" reset, which she initially metabolizes as freedom (ASM #606) but which becomes a slower-burning exposure when Peter's intermittent sentimentality keeps puncturing the no-strings frame she negotiated.
- MacKay-run scenes in which Odessa Drake reads her accurately; Felicia tolerates this because Odessa is structurally a peer and a woman, and the exposure does not carry the gendered-violation valence.

#### Escalation curve

- **T+0 to T+minutes:** The verbal repertoire shifts. Quips become sharper, more cutting, with an edge of contempt that is unusual for her — the contempt is targeted at the *exposing party*, but its real function is to re-establish frame control by making the witness flinch. If you make them recoil, they were not really seeing you; they were reacting to you. The polarity is reversed and safety is partially restored.
- **T+minutes to T+hours:** Physical exit. Felicia leaves. She is not a stay-and-fight-it-out partner in conflict; she removes herself from the witnessed space and reconstitutes alone. This is sometimes mistaken for avoidance writ small; it is actually frame-reset behavior, and she will return when she has re-established control over what is visible.
- **T+hours to T+days:** Compensatory performance. She executes a high-visibility, high-control operation — a heist, a seduction, a public theft — that re-establishes her as the *author* of the frame in front of audiences. This is not childish acting-out; it is functional self-repair, and it works.
- **T+days to T+weeks:** *If* the exposing witness was a primary attachment, the exposure axis cross-links with the attachment axis (§7.4) and escalation continues. *If* the witness was peripheral, recovery completes here.

#### Behavioral signature in decompensated state

- Speech becomes more *literary* — references multiply, the verbal mask thickens. Where stable-Felicia is casually witty, exposed-Felicia is constructedly witty; the difference is detectable but subtle.
- Wardrobe becomes more dramatic. She dresses more visibly, including in civilian contexts, recruiting the visual frame to do the work the verbal frame can no longer fully carry.
- The luck-power deployment (when she had it) became more reflexive and less calibrated under this state — a tell that the field was being used as an emotional regulator, not just a tool. The post-Strange period removed the tell but the underlying pattern persists; in its current absence, she over-deploys agility flourishes (unnecessary acrobatics in approaches, the gratuitous flip-and-land entry) that serve the same function.
- Eye contact extends *past* social norms — the hold-and-don't-blink that converts being-seen into seeing-back. This is a learned trick; you can date it to the post-rape training period.

#### Recovery profile

Fast (hours to days) if the exposing witness is not a primary attachment. Indefinite if they are.

---

### 7.4 The Attachment Axis: Primary-Bond Loss or Sentimental Violation

#### Trigger profile

Loss, betrayal, withdrawal, or *unwanted sentimentality* from a primary attachment. The fourth item is the most counterintuitive and the most operationally important: Felicia decompensates not only from a partner withdrawing but from a partner *deepening* a bond she has framed as casual. The Waid-era ASM #606 sequence is the cleanest example — she negotiates the reconnection with Peter on explicit no-strings terms, and his subsequent affective intrusion is experienced as a contract breach, producing the sharp withdrawal and hostility that characterized that arc.

The hierarchy of attachment figures across the canon:
1. Walter Hardy (father) — idealized, intermittently present, the iconography donor.
2. Peter Parker / Spider-Man — the longitudinal primary, the partner against whom all subsequent partners are measured.
3. The Black Fox — surrogate paternal/mentor, especially in the MacKay run.
4. Bruno, Doctor Korpse, the in-crew figures — the chosen family, latterly elevated to near-primary status.
5. Odessa Drake — peer-rival-intimate, a relationship Felicia has never quite categorized, which is itself diagnostic.

#### Escalation curve

- **T+0 to T+hours:** The devaluation pivot. Whoever the attachment figure is, Felicia begins constructing a contemptuous frame around them. "He was always going to —" "She never really —" The contempt is a defense against the felt loss; the speed of its construction is proportional to the depth of the bond.
- **T+hours to T+days:** Rebound engagement. She seeks a new partner, ally, or operation that explicitly figures the displaced attachment. Working for the Foreigner in *Web of Spider-Man* #6 immediately post-Peter is the template — *use the new partner to metabolize the old*. The rebound partner is often structurally inferior to the lost attachment, which is the point: the inferiority guarantees the new bond cannot threaten the framework.
- **T+days to T+weeks:** Compulsive risk-seeking. Operations chosen during this window are larger, more elaborate, more theatrical — and notably less *needed*. The MacKay run shows several heists that are diagnostically excessive in this register, executed when she is metabolizing some attachment event happening in parallel.
- **T+weeks to T+months:** If the loss is not metabolized — and metabolization requires the attachment figure to *return and accept the wounded state*, see §5 — the structure begins to ossify. The cold operational mode consolidates; the in-group shrinks; the ethical perimeter tightens (rarely loosens here, in contrast to the humiliation axis — she becomes more rule-bound, not less, because rules are a substitute for the lost relational scaffold).

#### Behavioral signature in decompensated state

- Sleep architecture: this is the one axis where her vegetative regulation actually shifts. Onset latency extends; she works later, drinks slightly more in the late evenings, reads in bed past three. Mid-cycle waking increases.
- Aesthetic acquisition behavior intensifies. The pattern of buying or stealing beautiful objects she does not need spikes in this state — she is filling a relational vacancy with sensory input. The objects acquired tend toward the *paired*: a matched set of earrings, twin sculptures, a diptych. The unconscious symbolism is unmistakable.
- Verbal references to the lost attachment increase under the guise of casual mention. She is one of those people who, in the presence of a third party, will produce the name of the absent figure twice in a conversation, both times framed as throwaway, neither time actually throwaway.
- Sexual contact with the rebound partner shows shorter total duration, fewer repeats, lower kissing-frequency-to-other-contact ratio than her baseline with a chosen partner. She is going through motions she designed for herself.

#### Recovery profile

The slowest and most variable of the three axes. Pure-loss decompensations (the attachment figure is dead, gone, or genuinely unreachable) can take years, and some are never fully metabolized — Peter is, in a real sense, a wound she has been managing since her mid-twenties and which the canon has never permitted to close. Sentimentality-violation decompensations recover faster, often when the violating partner accepts the original frame and stops intruding affectively.

---

### 7.5 The Compound Failure: When Axes Cross-Link

The *Superior Spider-Man* sequence (SSM #20 through the early issues of *Amazing Spider-Man* vol. 3) is the documented worst case and warrants close reading because it illustrates how the three axes interact.

The Otto event delivered:
- **Humiliation axis:** male body overpowering hers, dislocated jaw, witnessable damage, no authored frame.
- **Exposure axis:** the beating happened in the costume, in her professional context, in front of her peer reputation. The frame she had built around Spider-Man-as-partner-or-tolerated-antagonist shattered into a frame in which Spider-Man is an abuser.
- **Attachment axis:** the perpetrator wore the face and body of the longitudinal primary. She had no way, at the time, to distinguish the impostor; her felt experience was *Peter did this*. The attachment figure was simultaneously lost (by becoming the perpetrator) and confirmed as exactly the kind of threat the original index trauma trained her to expect.

All three axes triggered simultaneously, and the compensated structure could not absorb the combined load. The resulting decompensation was the longest, deepest, and most ethically permissive of her recorded canon: organized-crime escalation, attempted murder of Spider-Man, the cold mode sustained over multiple arcs, the perimeter eroded to its furthest extent.

What is diagnostically reassuring is the *recovery*. The Spencer-era arcs walk this back gradually — she returns to thieving, returns to the playful affect, returns to the ethical perimeter, returns (cautiously) to a workable relationship with Peter. The MacKay run finds her more integrated than she has ever been. The compound failure did not destroy the structure; it forced a rebuild, and the rebuild is, by the available evidence, marginally sturdier than the original.

---

### 7.6 Sub-Decompensation Patterns: The Tells Before the Break

For surveillance purposes, the following micro-indicators reliably precede full decompensation by 24–96 hours and are present across all three axes:

- **The unfunny quip.** A wisecrack delivered with correct cadence and incorrect timing — landing a half-beat early or late. The verbal machinery is running on autopilot while affect is reorganizing underneath.
- **Wardrobe over-determination.** A noticeable up-shift in the dramatic register of civilian dress: heels where flats would do, a coat with a silhouette, a piece of jewelry visibly chosen. She is recruiting the visual frame because the affective frame is slipping.
- **Increased solo operation.** Where stable-Felicia works increasingly with her crew, pre-decompensation Felicia begins to peel jobs off for herself. The crew is being protected from a state she does not want them to witness, *and* the solitary operation is a frame-control exercise.
- **The shorter touch.** Greeting contact (the hand on the arm, the brief hug) abbreviates by 200–400 milliseconds. Almost imperceptible; entirely reliable.
- **Compulsive aesthetic intake.** Gallery visits, perfume purchases, deliberate cooking, late-night reading. She is dosing herself with non-relational beauty because relational regulation is destabilizing.
- **The increased mention of the father.** Walter Hardy's name surfaces in conversation more frequently in pre-decompensation periods, usually in a wry or distancing register. The original idealized attachment is being touched for stabilization.

---

### 7.7 What Will Not Break Her

Equally worth documenting, because the surveillance error in the opposite direction is to over-predict collapse. Felicia is *not* destabilized by:

- Physical injury per se, including serious injury, provided the structural conditions of §7.2 are absent.
- Financial loss. She has stolen and re-stolen fortunes; money does not load her self-concept.
- Public exposure of her criminal identity. This channel is pre-burned.
- Loss of secondary attachments. Acquaintances die, allies depart, marks she liked turn out to be worse than expected — she absorbs these with the standard ironic register and moves on.
- Conflict with female peers, including hostile conflict. The gendered-overpowering circuit is not activated; she fights women without the index-trauma loading and recovers normally.
- Operational failure. She has failed heists, been outsmarted, lost to Spider-Man, lost to police. Failure is metabolized inside the craft frame and produces refinement, not collapse.
- Solitude. She is a high-functioning solitary; extended periods alone are restorative, not stressful.

The surveillance summary: she is a narrow-spectrum decompensator. Most of what would break a comparable operator does not touch her. What touches her touches her precisely, and along three identifiable rails, and the tells are present 24–96 hours in advance for a watcher who knows what they are looking at.

---

### 7.8 Prognostic Note

The longitudinal trajectory across forty-plus years of canon shows a slow, real consolidation. Each compound failure has produced a sturdier rebuild. The MacKay-era stabilization — crew, ethos, integrated relationship to her own past, tolerable handling of the Peter relationship — represents the most resilient configuration on file. The failure modes documented above remain live; the structure remains, by clinical standards, *compensated* rather than *resolved*. But the direction of travel is unambiguous, and the rate, while glacial, is positive.

A subject who has rebuilt herself this many times has acquired a meta-skill — *the ability to rebuild* — that is itself protective. The decompensations will recur. They will be shorter, shallower, and better-recovered each time. This is what trauma-organized adults look like when the organization is genuinely working.

— UATU, Section 7 ends.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU DOSSIER — FELICIA HARDY (BLACK CAT)
## Section 9: Trajectory & Forward Assessment

---

### 9.1 Where the Curve Is Pointing

The longitudinal slope, taken across forty-plus years of behavioral data, is **gently positive, with a wide variance band**. The Felicia of 1979 — engineering a prison break in costume to court a father she had constructed in absentia — and the Felicia of the post-MacKay era — running a competent crew, mentoring younger thieves, holding a tolerable working memory of her own past — are recognizably the same operator running the same software, but the software has been patched. The patches are real. They are also fragile.

What the trend line predicts, if extrapolated unperturbed, is a continued slow integration: more crew, more chosen-family structure, more aesthetic mastery, fewer acute decompensations, longer intervals between identity-collapses, gradually thinning utility of the mask. She is, in the actuarial sense, *aging into* a version of herself that the nineteen-year-old who built Black Cat would not have predicted and would, with some embarrassment, approve of.

But trend lines do not survive shocks, and her file is unusually rich in the kinds of shocks she does not handle well. The forward assessment must therefore be done in branches.

---

### 9.2 The Open Questions

These are the genuinely unresolved variables — the ones whose answers will determine which branch she lives down.

**a. Can she sustain a relationship with a man she is not in costume around?** Not "will she" — she has, sporadically, with the civilian Peter and with Flash — but *sustain*. Every depicted attempt has terminated at the moment the partner stops being a stranger. The open question is whether the recent MacKay-era softening represents a real capacity expansion or merely a longer fuse on the same charge.

**b. What does she become when she stops being physically peerless?** Her counterphobic architecture is *embodied*. Athletic decline — even modest, even survivable — strikes directly at the original anti-helplessness organization. She is now well into her fourth depicted decade of operational life; the gear is still there, but the question of what Felicia is when the body finally argues back is unanswered because she has never let herself imagine the answer.

**c. Will the in-group hold?** Bruno, the Black Fox, Doctor Korpse, the connections to Odessa Drake and the Thieves Guild — this is the most genuinely sustaining structure she has ever built. It is also a structure of criminals, with the attrition rates that implies. The death or betrayal of a single core member would be a stress event of a magnitude she has not previously been tested at, because she has never previously had this much to lose.

**d. Does she ever go straight, in any meaningful sense?** The honest answer is probably no, and probably it would be a mistake if she did — the craft is where her selfhood lives. But the related question is whether she can develop a *civilian shell* (legitimate identity, declared assets, a public-facing self that is not a forgery) that lets her live in daylight. Nothing in the file says she has tried.

**e. Children — wanted, refused, or simply un-considered?** Canon has been silent. The silence itself is data: she has not depicted ambivalence, which suggests the question has been pre-foreclosed rather than worked through. A pre-foreclosed question is a fork point waiting to happen.

**f. What is her relationship to the Walter Hardy mythology now that she has surpassed him?** She built her identity around being his daughter and his rescuer. She is now the more accomplished thief and the head of a more functional crew. The narcissistic-injury fuel of the father-idealization has burned down. What replaces it as the organizing myth?

**g. Does the index trauma ever get spoken aloud, to anyone, outside a crisis?** The Smith arc let her say it because the perpetrator had returned and the plot required it. She has not, in available canon, told it as autobiography to an intimate during peacetime. Until she does, the compensation remains compensation.

---

### 9.3 Fork Points

A *fork point* in this file is a specific class of event that will, with high probability, route her toward growth or toward catastrophe and is unlikely to leave her unchanged. They are listed in approximate order of how likely they are to occur and how decisive they would be.

**Fork 1 — A second sexual assault, attempted or completed.** The single most dangerous event imaginable for her structure. The first one *built* Black Cat; a second would either consolidate her into a far colder, far more lethal operator (the post-Otto trajectory writ permanent) or — under conditions of immediate support from her in-group — would force the long-deferred work of actually metabolizing the original. The variable that decides the branch is whether someone she trusts is *physically present in the aftermath*. Alone, she goes cold. Held, she might finally cry.

**Fork 2 — Peter Parker's death, public knowledge.** She has organized a great deal of her interior life around the *possibility* of him, even when actively avoiding him. His removal as a horizon would force her either to (a) collapse into a brief, ugly grief and emerge with the Peter-shaped scaffolding finally cleared, freeing her for an adult choice of partner, or (b) sublimate the loss into a new mythology — *the woman who loved the hero* — which would calcify her permanently into a romanticized half-life. Branch depends on how busy her crew keeps her in the first six weeks.

**Fork 3 — A protégé chooses her as a maternal figure explicitly and demands more.** The mentor role with Bruno and others has been comfortable because the protégés have not asked her for what she did not get. A younger thief — particularly a young woman with a recognizable trauma — naming her as the mother-substitute and asking for *protection during her own crisis* would activate the deepest reparative material in Felicia's psyche. She is more likely to grow under this pressure than under any romantic one. The risk is that she over-identifies and re-injures herself in the process.

**Fork 4 — Forced unmasking in a venue she cannot manage.** Tabloid exposure, federal indictment in true name, a metahuman event that strips the costume in front of cameras — anything that takes the mask away without her consent. This is the pressure point that has the longest history of producing brittle grandiosity. The growth branch requires that her in-group hold around her and that she be allowed to *rebuild a public self on her own terms*; the catastrophe branch is a hard pivot into the organized-crime mode last seen post-Superior, possibly permanent.

**Fork 5 — Walter Hardy's actual, final death (rather than the various near-misses).** The end of the father-myth. Growth branch: she becomes her own author for the first time, possibly retires the Black Cat name or radically redesigns it. Catastrophe branch: she enacts a heist of such operatic scale, in his memory, that she gets herself imprisoned or killed honoring a ghost.

**Fork 6 — A serious, non-survivable-without-help physical injury.** A break that does not heal cleanly, a concussion sequela, a knee that ends the gymnastics. The forced confrontation with her own body's finitude. Growth branch: she discovers that the crew, the craft, the mind, and even the partner of her choosing will stay — that she was loved, not merely watched. Catastrophe branch: cosmetic and pharmacological compensation, increasingly reckless ops to prove the body still works, an acceleration toward a final job.

**Fork 7 — Pregnancy, planned or otherwise.** Almost entirely unmodeled in canon. The branch matrix is unusually wide: termination handled privately and folded into existing structure (most likely, most stable); carried to term with a co-parent (would require a relational reorganization she has never demonstrated); carried to term alone (the reparative father-and-daughter mythology reversed and re-enacted, with all the risk and possibility that implies). This is the fork point with the highest *transformative* potential and the lowest predictive certainty.

**Fork 8 — A genuine offer of legitimate work at her actual skill level.** Security consultancy, museum acquisitions, the SHIELD-adjacent grey-economy roles that her competence would command. She has never been seriously tested by the offer of going straight *at no loss of status or excitement*. The growth branch is that she takes a hybrid path. The catastrophe branch is sneering refusal followed by a months-long bender of escalating heists to prove she was not tempted — which would tell us she was.

---

### 9.4 What Pushes Her Toward Growth

The growth vectors are unglamorous and consistent. They are also already in her life, in seed form.

- **The crew, kept alive and kept honest.** Every day Bruno and the Black Fox and Korpse stay above ground and stay loyal, she accumulates evidence that attachment is survivable. This is the single most therapeutic structure she has, and it is not labeled as such, which is why it works.
- **Mentorship demand from below.** Being needed by a younger operator forces her to articulate the ethical code she has long held implicitly, and articulation is the front edge of integration.
- **Aesthetic projects that are not heists.** Art collection in earnest, patronage, possibly the financing of legitimate restorations of pieces she has previously stolen and returned. Anything that lets the aesthetic self exist without the crime as alibi.
- **A therapist she cannot run game on.** Vanishingly improbable that she ever sits in an office, but the functional equivalent — an older woman, perhaps in the criminal milieu, perhaps adjacent to it, who has seen her exactly and refuses to be charmed — would do the work. Madame Masque is the wrong shape; an older retired thief, a wartime survivor, a Thieves Guild elder is closer.
- **Telling the story.** Once, to one person, in peacetime. The Smith-era confession was extracted under duress. A volunteered telling, in a quiet room, to someone who will not flinch and will not perform sympathy, is the milestone that would mark genuine integration. It need not be Peter. It probably should not be Peter.
- **Repeated, low-stakes practice at being seen unstyled.** A morning a week with no costume, no makeup, no operational frame, in the company of someone who has nothing to gain. This is the rep work of which she has done very little.
- **Loss survived without collapse.** Each non-catastrophic loss she metabolizes — a job that fails, a peer who dies of natural causes, a romance that ends with handshake rather than betrayal — broadens her tolerable affect band. The slope of the long arc is built from these.

---

### 9.5 What Pushes Her Toward Catastrophe

The catastrophe vectors are concentrated and recognizable. The file has seen them before.

- **Sexual humiliation, particularly public.** Re-evokes the index trauma and the structure has no developed channel for it; the response is cold operational mode and escalation. Highest single risk factor for permanent character calcification.
- **A male figure she has been managing physically overpowering her.** Otto already ran this experiment; the result was the organized-crime pivot. A repetition would be harder to walk back, because the demonstration that the counterphobic compensation is *contingent* would be doubled. Two data points make a trend in her interior.
- **Discovery that a sustaining relationship was, all along, a manipulation.** A crew member revealed as an asset of an enemy; a lover revealed as a long-running con; the luck-powers shame structure replayed at a higher amplitude. Brittle grandiosity, predatory affect, and a willingness to use lethal force she normally avoids.
- **Isolation.** She decompensates alone. A period — six months, a year — without the crew, without an adversary worth her game, without an aesthetic project, is more dangerous to her than any active enemy. Boredom is a fork point in itself.
- **Substance discovery in middle adulthood.** No history, but the behavioral-addiction profile is real and the substitution risk under a body-decline scenario is non-trivial. Stimulants to maintain the edge, then anxiolytics to come down, then a problem. Watch for it; it would not be the obvious vector but it would be the efficient one.
- **A heist she pulls *because* it might kill her.** The slow-suicide-as-virtuoso-performance pathway. Career criminals of her caliber sometimes drift here in late career; the file does not show it yet, but the conditions for it (the body argument, the loss of a Peter-shaped horizon, an in-group collapse) are convergence-prone.
- **Becoming the thing she courted.** The Kingpin role, the Odessa Drake role, the throne of an organization. She has the talent and, under injury, the appetite. The catastrophe is not that she would be bad at it; it is that she would be good at it and would lose the ethical code that is the load-bearing wall of her selfhood.

---

### 9.6 Specific Predictions, Time-Indexed

Where the file permits, with the standard caveats.

**Short horizon (one to three operational years).** Continued crew-based operation; one or two acute Spider-Man re-engagements, increasingly bracketed and post-romantic in tone; a major heist at the scale that earns press; at least one fork-point event from the list above, probably Fork 3 or Fork 4 — a protégé crisis or a partial exposure. Predicted outcome: net positive, with one ugly month somewhere in the middle.

**Medium horizon (five to ten operational years).** A genuine relational test — either a sustained partnership with a non-Peter figure who can hold her without being charmed, or a final, decisive renunciation of the Peter horizon. Likely articulation of the in-group as a chosen family in some explicit way (a will, a contingency, a recorded promise). First serious bodily limit acknowledged. Possible legitimate-cover business established, almost certainly an aesthetic concern.

**Long horizon (the back third of the life).** Two stable branches and one wild card. Stable A: the retired-master who runs the crew from a distance, mentors, curates her stolen-and-returned collection, lives well, tells the story finally and to the right person. Stable B: the Guild figure, formalized, less playful, more weighty, an institutional presence in the criminal aesthetic economy. Wild card: she dies on a job she chose because the job was *worth* dying on, by her own aesthetic, and the dossier closes with the observation that she scripted even the ending.

---

### 9.7 The Single Most Important Variable

If only one factor were available to predict her long arc, it would not be the romantic, the criminal, or the somatic. It would be **whether the in-group survives intact through the next major shock.** Everything else in her psychology has been tested across decades and is, within tolerances, known. The chosen-family structure is the one genuinely new variable in her file, the one piece of architecture that postdates the original trauma-organization, and the one resource capable of carrying her through events that, alone, she has historically failed.

Protect the crew, and the rest of the file bends toward integration. Lose the crew, and the file bends toward the cold version of her that has always been latent and has, twice now, briefly shown its face.

The benevolent reading of this dossier — the one consistent with the spirit of the project — is that she has done, with what she was given, more than was reasonable to expect, and that the work remaining is not corrective but elaborative. She is not a problem to be solved. She is a long arc still being written, by herself, on her own terms, and the most useful thing an observer can do is mark the fork points clearly and stay out of the room.

— *UATU, file open, watch continuing.*
